## General Property Configuration of Charts
<div>
          <p>
            The supOS platform enables you to configure charts in business
            designer through scripts, which can be helpful when the provided
            configuration items do not meet your requirements.
          </p>
        </div>
        <article
          className="nested1"
          aria-labelledby="concept_wk3_wmc_hvb__title_xk3_wmc_hvb"
          id="concept_wk3_wmc_hvb"
        >

### General Script

<div>

:::info

The following examples do not include all supported configuration items. You can go to https://api.highcharts.com.cn/highcharts/index.html to check all items.

:::

<ul id="concept_n2b_5mc_hvb__ul_ddw_plc_hvb">
              <li>
                <strong>updateConfigNew</strong>
              </li>
            </ul>
            <pre>
              <code>
                {"  "}/**{"\n"} * @desc: General packed functions to change
                charts property{"\n"} * @param {"{"}String{"}"} property:
                Property level{"\n"} * @param {"{"}String{"}"} serviceName:
                Property value{"\n"} */{"\n"}
                {"  "}var chart = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                Id');{"\n"}
                {"  "}chart.updateConfigNew('chart-&gt;options3d-&gt;enabled',
                true);
              </code>
            </pre>
            <ul id="concept_n2b_5mc_hvb__ul_prm_rlc_hvb">
              <li>
                <strong>deleteAllSeries</strong>
              </li>
            </ul>
            <pre>
              <code>
                {"  "}/**{"\n"} * @desc: Packed function to clear all series on
                current chart{"\n"} */{"\n"}
                {"  "}var chart = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                Id');{"\n"}
                {"  "}chart.deleteAllSeries();
              </code>
            </pre>
            <ul id="concept_n2b_5mc_hvb__ul_shq_rlc_hvb">
              <li>
                <strong>getCurrentInstance</strong>
              </li>
            </ul>
            <pre>
              <code>
                {" "}
                /**{"\n"} * @desc Packed function to get highchart instance,
                used to call embedded highchart function{"\n"} * @return {"{"}
                Object{"}"}: Highchart object{"\n"} */{"\n"}
                {"  "}var chart = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                Id');{"\n"}
                {"  "}var hchart = chart.getCurrentInstance();{"\n"}
                {"  "}// add a data entry{"\n"}
                {"  "}hchart.addSeries({"{"}
                {"\n"}
                {"  "}name: 'name',{"\n"}
                {"  "}data: [{"\n"}
                {"    "}
                {"{"} y: 123, name: 'Emma' {"}"},{"\n"}
                {"    "}
                {"{"} y: 123, name: 'Jason' {"}"},{"\n"}
                {"  "}]{"\n"}
                {"}"})
              </code>
            </pre>
          </div>
        </article>
      </article>

        className="nested0"
        aria-labelledby="ariaid-title10"
        id="free_layout"
      >

<code>
// set data for video carousel{"\n"}
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom("component
                  id").setStreamSource({"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}carousel: false, // whether to run video carousel{"\n"}
                  {"  "}maxchannel: null, // maximum number of channels{"\n"}
                  {"  "}chooseChannel: undefined, // select a channel{"\n"}
                  {"  "}cameramodel: null, // video mode{"\n"}
                  {"  "}manufacturer: null, // manufacturer{"\n"}
                  {"  "}videoSource: "", // video source data{"\n"}
                  {"}"});{"\n"}// set data for real-time playback{"\n"}
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom("component
                  id").setHistorySource({"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}videoSource: "", // video source data{"\n"}
                  {"}"});
                </code>

                  primitiveType:"DOUBLE"{"}"},{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"{"}{" "}
                  color:"#39435A",name:"system:Template_2:aa_5:system:Property_19",
                  primitiveType:"FLOAT"{"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}]{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// get the element with an ID as TrendChart-1{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var TrendChart1 =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('TrendChart-1'); {"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// display too;bar{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setToolBarShow(true);{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// select list type{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setShowListType("2");{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// background color{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setDivBackgroundColor('red');{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// chart color{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setChartBackgroundColor('red');{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// border color{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setBorderColor('red');{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// clider color{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setCrosshairColor('red');{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// font color{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setTextColor('red');{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// add data source (less than 8 entries are allowed to
                  insert and excessed data is invalid){"\n"}
                  {"  "}// single data source{"{"}
                  {"}"} multple data source[] name&amp;primitiveType&amp;color
                  are required{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setObjectData(obj){"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// set starting time{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.setRegularTime(start,end);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}// change time and data source (up to 8 entries) at the
                  same time{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.changeTimeAndSource(start, end, type,
                  dataSourceObj);{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}/* ************following examples are for
                  changeTimeAndSource************ */{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// no data source repalcement, no time-&gt;call
                  setRegularTime-&gt;prompts no start/end time and no subsequent
                  operation{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.changeTimeAndSource();{"\n"}
                  {"  "}// no data source repalcement, start time-&gt;call
                  setRegularTime-&gt;prompts no start/end time and no subsequent
                  operation{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.changeTimeAndSource('2019-10-16 08:30:00')
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// no data source repalcement, end time-&gt;call
                  setRegularTime-&gt;prompts no start/end time and no subsequent
                  operation{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.changeTimeAndSource(undefined,'2019-10-16
                  08:30:00'){"\n"}
                  {"  "}// no data source repalcement, start time-&gt;call
                  setRegularTime-&gt;replace time period of current trend chart
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.changeTimeAndSource('2019-10-16
                  08:30:00','2019-10-16 08:30:30'){"\n"}
                  {"  "}// data source repalcement (object)-&gt;replace time
                  period of current trend chart and data source{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var obj = {"{"} color:"#009DD7",name:"mock_demo:mock1",
                  primitiveType:"Float"{"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.changeTimeAndSource('2019-10-16
                  08:30:00','2019-10-16 08:30:30','all',obj){"\n"}
                  {"  "}// data source repalcement (array)-&gt;replace time
                  period of current trend chart and data source{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.changeTimeAndSource('2019-10-16
                  08:30:00','2019-10-16 08:30:30','all',obj){"\n"}
                  {"  "}// data source repalcement (array), no time-&gt;prompts
                  no start/end time and no subsequent operation{"\n"}
                  {"  "}TrendChart1.changeTimeAndSource('dfd','2019-10-16
                  08:30:30','all', obj)
                </code>
              </pre>
            </div>
          </article>
        </article>

            <div>
              <p>Data format</p>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  [{"\n"}
                  {"    "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}value: 'todo', //
                  todo/done/request/attention/delegate/{"\n"}
                  {"        "}label: 'to-do',{"\n"}
                  {"        "}isShow: true, // whether to display it{"\n"}
                  {"        "}children: [ // table content{"\n"}
                  {"            "}
                  {"{"} {"\n"}
                  {"                "}label: 'index', {"\n"}
                  {"                "}value: 'index', {"\n"}
                  {"                "}isShow: true, // whether to display the
                  item{"\n"}
                  {"                "}showModal: false, // click to display
                  pop-up{"\n"}
                  {"                "}url: '', // propmt url{"\n"}
                  {"                "}modalWidth: 1200, // prompt width{"\n"}
                  {"                "}modalHeight: 800, // prompt height{"\n"}
                  {"                "}style: {"{"} {"\n"}
                  {"                    "}color: '#000', // item style{"\n"}
                  {"                    "}fontSize: 14,{"\n"}
                  {"                    "}fontFamily: 'Arial'{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}
                  {"}"},{"\n"}
                  {"            "}...{"\n"}
                  {"        "}]{"\n"}
                  {"    "}
                  {"}"},{"\n"}
                  {"    "}...{"\n"}]
                </code>
              </pre>
            </div>
          </article>

              Example Code
            </h3>
            <div>
              <p>Data format</p>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}// get element with an Id as htDiv-k8tj6ada0-704{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var reporterCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('htDiv-k8tj6ada0-704');{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// component name{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setFormItemId('ReporterCtrl');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const reporterName = reporterCtrl.getFormItemId();{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// fill type{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setFillDataType('replace');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const fillDataType = reporterCtrl.getFillDataType();
                  {"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}//{"  "}scroll bar{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setScrollbarVisible('auto');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const scrollbarVisible =
                  reporterCtrl.getScrollbarVisible();{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// fix on top{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setPosition('topEnable', true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const topEnable =
                  reporterCtrl.getPosition()['topEnable'];{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// fix on bottom{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setPosition('bottomEnable', true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const bottomEnable =
                  reporterCtrl.getPosition()['bottomEnable'];{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// fix on left{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setPosition('leftEnable', true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const leftEnable =
                  reporterCtrl.getPosition()['leftEnable'];{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}// fix on right{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setPosition('rightEnable', true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const rightEnable =
                  reporterCtrl.getPosition()['rightEnable'];{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}//{"  "}run edit {"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setRunTimeEdit(true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const runTimeEdit = reporterCtrl.getRunTimeEdit();{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}//{"  "}zoom out{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setRunTimeZoomSheet(true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const runTimeZoomSheet =
                  reporterCtrl.getRunTimeZoomSheet();{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}//{"  "}zoom in{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setRunTimeZoomLargeSheet(true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const runTimeZoomLargeSheet =
                  reporterCtrl.getRunTimeZoomLargeSheet();{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}//{"  "}Sheet page{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setRunTimeShowSheet(true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const runTimeShowSheet =
                  reporterCtrl.getRunTimeShowSheet();{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}//{"  "}initial load{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setInitLoadData(true);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const initLoadData = reporterCtrl.getInitLoadData();
                  {"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}//{"  "}background color{"\n"}
                  {"  "}reporterCtrl.setBackgroundColor('#f5f5f5');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}const backgroundColor =
                  reporterCtrl.getBackgroundColor();
                </code>

                  {"  "}// set to obkect {"{"}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}

                  {"  "}// set values in batches through component name{"\n"}

                  'labelValue', component name 2: 'labelValue2' {"}"})

                  Id');{"\n"}var value = HiddenField.getValue();{"\n"}// get

                  2']);

                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}SelectCtrl.getValue();

              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}var SelectCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}SelectCtrl.setValue('1');
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_1618152042__ul_vzh_11s_hvb">
                <li>Import options</li>
              </ul>
              <div className="note note_note">
              

:::info

Only works when set data source to static under property.

:::

</div>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {" "}
                  var data = [{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}optionText: 'M', {"\n"}
                  {"        "}optionValue: '1'{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"}"},{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}optionText: 'F',{"\n"}
                  {"        "}optionValue: '2'{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}];{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var SelectCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}SelectCtrl.setObjectData(data);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_1618152042__ul_rdp_51s_hvb">
                <li>Set whether to enable multiple selections</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}var SelectCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}SelectCtrl.setIsMultiple(true);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_1618152042__ul_dwt_51s_hvb">
                <li>Get form data</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"   "}// Get component value in batches after submitting
                  forms{"\n"}
                  {"   "}// formItemId is component name [component name 1,
                  component name 2]{"\n"}
                  {"   "}scriptUtil.getFormData([formItemId]);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_1618152042__ul_ik5_51s_hvb">
                <li>Set form data</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"   "}// Set data in batches to change form data at once
                  {"\n"}
                  {"   "}// formItemId is component namevalue is component
                  value{"\n"}
                  {"   "}scriptUtil.setFormData({"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"     "}'formItemId'value{"\n"}
                  {"   "}
                  {"}"});{"\n"}
                </code>
              </pre>

              <ul id="unique_330311629__ul_r2k_p5q_hvb">
                <li>Set data source</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}// data format{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var data = [{"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"    "}value: 'zhejiang',{"\n"}
                  {"    "}label: 'Zhejiang',{"\n"}
                  {"    "}children: [{"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"      "}value: 'hangzhou',{"\n"}
                  {"      "}label: 'Hangzhou',{"\n"}
                  {"      "}children: [{"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}value: 'xihu',{"\n"}
                  {"        "}label: 'West Lake'{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"}"}]{"\n"}
                  {"    "}
                  {"}"}]{"\n"}
                  {"  "}
                  {"}"}, {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"    "}value: 'jiangsu',{"\n"}
                  {"    "}label: 'Jiangsu',{"\n"}
                  {"    "}children: [{"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"      "}value: 'nanjing',{"\n"}
                  {"      "}label: 'Nanjing',{"\n"}
                  {"      "}children: [{"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}value: 'zhonghuamen',{"\n"}
                  {"        "}label: 'Zhong Hua Men'{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"}"}]{"\n"}
                  {"    "}
                  {"}"}]{"\n"}
                  {"  "}
                  {"}"}];{"\n"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}var Cascader = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                  Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}// import data source{"\n"}
                  {"  "}Cascader.setImportData(data)
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_330311629__ul_z4c_q5q_hvb">
                <li>Get component value</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}var Cascader = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                  Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var value = Cascader.getChooseOption()
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_330311629__ul_vgh_11s_hvb">
                <li>Set component value</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}var Cascader = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                  Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var vals = ['zhejiang','hangzhou','xihu']{"\n"}
                  {"  "}Cascader.setValue(vals)
                </code>
              </pre>

              </ul>

                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}var Cascader = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                  Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var res = Cascader.getValid(); // true or false{"\n"}
                </code>

                  {"   "}var RadioCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}RadioCtrl.getValue();

                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}var RadioCtrl =

                  {"  "}RadioCtrl.setValue('XX');
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_1990928856__ul_vgh_11s_hvb">
                <li>Set data</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}var data = [{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}optionText: 'M', {"\n"}
                  {"        "}optionValue: '1'{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"}"},{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}optionText: 'F',{"\n"}
                  {"        "}optionValue: '2'{"\n"}
                  {"      "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}];{"\n"} var RadioCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}{" "}
                  RadioCtrl.setObjectData(data);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_1990928856__ul_dwt_51s_hvb">
                <li>Get form data</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"   "}// Get component value in batches after submitting
                  forms{"\n"}
                  {"   "}// formItemId is component name [component name 1,
                  component name 2]{"\n"}
                  {"   "}scriptUtil.getFormData([formItemId]);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_1990928856__ul_ik5_51s_hvb">

              </ul>
              <pre>

                  {"   "}// Set data in batches to change form data at once
                  {"\n"}
                  {"   "}// formItemId is component namevalue is component
                  value{"\n"}
                  {"   "}scriptUtil.setFormData({"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"     "}'formItemId'value{"\n"}
                  {"   "}
                  {"}"});{"\n"}
                </code>

          <article
            className="nested2"
            aria-labelledby="unique_418701017__title_u4n_mcl_hvb"
            id="unique_418701017"
          >
            <h3
              className="topictitle3"
              id="unique_418701017__title_u4n_mcl_hvb"
            >
              Example Code
            </h3>
            <div>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_o4p_vqs_hvb">
                <li>Date data format</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}dateType: date, // date type includes date, time,
                  datetime, dateRange and datetimeRange{"\n"}format:
                  YYYY-MM-DD, // date format YYYY-MM-DD YYYY-M-D DD/MM/YYYY
                  and custom{"\n"}customFormat: {"\n"}
                  {"}"}
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_r2k_p5q_hvb">
                <li>Convert timestamp to date</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  // 2018-12-28 00:00:00{"\n"}
                  scriptUtil.timestampFormat(1545926400000, 'YYYY-MM-DD
                  HH:mm:ss');{"\n"}// 2018-12-28{"\n"}
                  scriptUtil.timestampFormat('1545926400000', 'YYYY-MM-DD');
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_z4c_q5q_hvb">
                <li>Convert date to timestamp</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  // 1543939200000{"\n"}
                  scriptUtil.timestampAntiFormat('2018-12-05');
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_vgh_11s_hvb">
                <li>Get selected date</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"\n"}var DatePicker =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}//
                  timestamp1545926400000{"\n"}DatePicker.getValue();
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_dwt_51s_hvb">
                <li>Set selected date</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  var DatePicker = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');
                  {"\n"}// timestamp{"\n"}DatePicker.setValue(1545926400000);{"\n"}
                  // date{"\n"}DatePicker.setValue(new Date());{"\n"}//
                  date string{"\n"}DatePicker.setValue('2018-12-01');{"\n"}//
                 date range{"\n"}DatePicker.setValue(['2018-10-10
                  10:10:10','2018-11-11 11:11:11']);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_ik5_51s_hvb">
                <li>Whether date passes verification</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  var DatePicker = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');
                  {"\n"}DatePicker.getValid();
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_brx_pzs_hvb">
                <li>Disable date selection</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  /{"\n"} *{"  "}@params {"{"}string{"}"} value disable date
                  e.g. '2018-10-10' with time'2018-10-10 10:10:10'{"\n"} *
                  {"  "}@params {"{"}string{"}"} type default is start:cannot
                  select date before end:cannot select date after{"\n"} */{"\n"}
                  var DatePicker = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                  Id');{"\n"}DatePicker.setDisabledDate('2018-01-01
                  10:10:10','start')
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_gw3_rzs_hvb">
                <li>Disable time selection</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  /{"\n"} *{"  "}@params {"{"}string{"}"} value disable time
                  e.g. '10:10:10'{"\n"} *{"  "}@params {"{"}string{"}"} type
                  default is start:cannot select time before end:cannot select
                  time after{"\n"} */{"\n"}var DatePicker =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  DatePicker.setDisabledTime('10:10:10','start')
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_dwt_51s_hv">
                <li>Get form data</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"   "}// Get component value in batches after submitting
                  forms{"\n"}
                  {"   "}// formItemId is component name [component name 1,
                  component name 2]{"\n"}
                  {"   "}scriptUtil.getFormData([formItemId]);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_418701017__ul_ik5_51s_h">
                <li>Set form data</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"   "}// Set data in batches to change form data at once
                  {"\n"}
                  {"   "}// formItemId is component namevalue is component
                  value{"\n"}
                  {"   "}scriptUtil.setFormData({"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"     "}'formItemId'value{"\n"}
                  {"   "}
                  {"}"});{"\n"}
                </code>
              </pre>

          <article
            className="nested2"
            aria-labelledby="unique_481608513__title_u4n_mcl_hvb"
            id="unique_481608513"
          >
            <h3
              className="topictitle3"
              id="unique_481608513__title_u4n_mcl_hvb"
            >
              Example Code
            </h3>
            <div>
              <ul id="unique_481608513__ul_t1y_cct_hvb">
                <li>Get tree node</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {" "}
                  var treeCtrl = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_481608513__ul_smr_dct_hvb">
                <li>Dynamic data source format</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"\n"}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"    "}list:[{"\n"}
                  {"        "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}id:'1',{"\n"}
                  {"            "}name:'parent 1',{"\n"}
                  {"            "}children:[{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"                    "}id:'1-1',{"\n"}
                  {"                    "}name:'child 1'{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}]{"\n"}
                  {"        "}
                  {"}"},{"\n"}
                  {"        "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}id:'2',{"\n"}
                  {"            "}name:'parent 2',{"\n"}
                  {"            "}children:[{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"                    "}id:'2-1',{"\n"}
                  {"                    "}name:'child 2'{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}]{"\n"}
                  {"        "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"    "}]{"\n"}
                  {"}"}
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_481608513__ul_sjv_2ct_hvb">
                <li>Set data</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}var treeCtrl = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                  Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var data = [{"\n"}
                  {"        "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}id:'1',{"\n"}
                  {"            "}name:'parent 1',{"\n"}
                  {"            "}children:[{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"                    "}id:'1-1',{"\n"}
                  {"                    "}name:'child 1'{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}]{"\n"}
                  {"        "}
                  {"}"},{"\n"}
                  {"        "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}id:'2',{"\n"}
                  {"            "}name:'parent 2',{"\n"}
                  {"            "}children:[{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"                    "}id:'2-1',{"\n"}
                  {"                    "}name:'child 2'{"\n"}
                  {"                "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"            "}]{"\n"}
                  {"        "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"    "}];{"\n"}
                  {"  "}treeCtrl.setImportData(data);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_481608513__ul_erp_fct_hvb">
                <li>Collapse a node by default</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"    "}var treeCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  {"    "}var keys = [ '1' ]{"\n"}
                  {"    "}treeCtrl.defaultExpandedKeys(keys);
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_481608513__ul_lpc_hct_hvb">
                <li>Select all parent nodes of the current selected node</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"    "}var treeCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  {"    "}treeCtrl.getParentNodes();{"\n"}
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_481608513__ul_zx4_3ct_hvb">
                <li>Manually refresh current data source</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"    "}var treeCtrl =
                  scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component Id');{"\n"}
                  {"    "}treeCtrl.reloadTreeData();{"\n"}
                </code>
              </pre>
            </div>

          <article
            className="nested2"
            aria-labelledby="unique_2034293453__title_u4n_mcl_hvb"
            id="unique_2034293453"
          >
            <h3
              className="topictitle3"
              id="unique_2034293453__title_u4n_mcl_hvb"
            >
              Example Code
            </h3>
            <div>
              <ul id="unique_2034293453__ul_t1y_cct_hvb">
                <li>Set table head</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  var table = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component id');
                  {"\n"}var columnHeader = [{"\n"}
                  {"  "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"    "}customName: 'index',{"\n"}
                  {"    "}originalName: '_index',{"\n"}
                  {"    "}align:'left',{"\n"}
                  {"    "}width: 100{"\n"}
                  {"  "}
                  {"}"},{"\n"}
                  {"  "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}

            <h3
              className="topictitle3"
              id="unique_179096636__title_u4n_mcl_hvb"
            >
              Example Code
            </h3>
            <div>
              <p>Set value</p>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}var instance = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                  Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var fileList = [{"\n"}
                  {"    "}
                  {"{"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}"fileDownloadUrl":
                  "/api/config/download?fileName=2022-03-09/1646832614807/file.png",
                  {"\n"}
                  {"        "}"fileName": "2022-03-09/1646832614807/upload
                  component.png"{"\n"}
                  {"    "}
                  {"}"}
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}]{"\n"}
                  {"  "}instance.setValue(fileList);{"\n"}
                  {"  "}// set data value in batches to change form data at once
                  {"\n"}
                  {"  "}scriptUtil.setFormData({"{"} 'component name 1':
                  fileList, 'component name 2': fileList {"}"})
                </code>
              </pre>
              <ul id="unique_179096636__ul_vlj_zmy_hvb">
                <li>Get value</li>
              </ul>
              <pre>
                <code>
                  {"  "}var instance = scriptUtil.getRegisterReactDom('component
                  Id');{"\n"}
                  {"  "}instance.getValue();{"\n"}
                  {"  "}// get element value by element name in batches{"\n"}
                  {"  "}var data = scriptUtil.getFormData(['component name
                  1','component name 2']);
                </code>
              </pre>
            </div>
